  export class $gd_kit_browser_live extends $mol_object {

    @ $mol_mem
    static hidden(next?: null) {
      if (next === undefined) this.hidden_handler()
      return this.doc().hidden ?? false
    }

    @ $mol_mem
    protected static hidden_handler() {
      return this.create_event(
        'visibilitychange',
        () => this.hidden(null),
        false
      )
    }
    protected static doc() {
      return this.$.$mol_dom_context.document
    }

    protected static create_event(
      name: Parameters<ReturnType<typeof this.doc>['addEventListener']>[0],
      cb: (e: Event) => void,
      useCapture?: boolean | AddEventListenerOptions
    ) {
      const doc = this.doc()
      const synced = $mol_wire_async(cb)
      doc.addEventListener(name, synced, useCapture)

      return { destructor: () => doc.removeEventListener(name, synced) }
    }

}

  class $gd_kit_entity2 extends $mol_object {
    constructor(
      readonly id: number
    ) { super() }

    defaults() {
      return {}
    }

    @ $mol_mem
    data( data?: ReturnType< this['defaults'] > ): ReturnType<this['defaults']> {
      return this.$.$mol_state_local.value(this.toString(), data) as ReturnType<this['defaults']> ?? this.defaults()
    }

    @ $mol_mem_key
    value<
      Field extends keyof ReturnType< this['data'] >
    >(
      field: Field,
      value?: ReturnType< this['data'] >[ Field ],
    ): ReturnType< this['data'] >[ Field ] {
      
      return this.data( value === undefined
        ? undefined
        : {
          ... this.data(),
          [ field ]: value,
        }
      )[ field as never ]
      
    }
  }

class $my_talent extends $my_entity {
  @ $mol_mem_key
  static factory(id: string) {
    return this.$.$my_talent.make({ id: () => id, })
  }

  @$mol_action
  static add(data: Partial<typeof $my_talent.defaults> ) {
     const talent = this.$.$my_talent.factory($mol_guid())

     talent.data(data)

    this.talent_ids( [... this.talent_ids(), talent.id() ] )
  }

    @$mol_mem
    static talent_ids(next?: readonly string[]) {
      return next ?? []
    }

  @$mol_action
  static search_ids(criteria: Partial<typeof $my_talent.defaults>) {
    return this.talent_ids().filter(id => compare(this.factory(id), criteria) )
  }

}

class $my_hero extends $my_entity {
  talent_ids(next?: readonly string[]) { return this.value('talent_ids', next) }
 
 @$mol_mem
  talents() { return this.talent_ids().map(id => this.$.my_talent.factory(id) ) }

  @$mol_action
  talent_add(talent_id: string ) {
    this.talent_ids( [... this.talent_ids(), talent_id ] )
  }

  talend_remove(id: string) { this.talend_ids( this.talend_ids().filter(talent_id => talent_id !== id ) ) }
}
